< Review>
Really enjoy doing business here. Friendly staff, clean environment, good inventory, and they offer receipts if you would like to itemize for medical expenses.

I like they offer a happy hour from 6am-10am and again from 2pm-6pm, rotating vendors with special deals and comps; and at times a discount table. Bring your own zipper bags from previous visits to save a new bag and a buck.

I'd recommend this place for the receipts alone, but overall for being upbeat with a positive vibe. Definitely one of my favorites!</Review>

<date>1478402776241< /date><Rating>2<//Rating>< Review>
TLDR:
No wait at prime time on Saturday night
Staff seemed confused and unorganized
Had to add salt to my dish, which I can't recall ever having done

I had higher expectations, but I suppose I should have known this wasn't really going to be the best when there wasn't a wait at prime dinner time on a Saturday night. Not to say the place wasn't busy. The hostess and servers seemed confused and not very organized. After our menus were brought, and man put water on the other end of the table from us, that we dragged towards our place settings. When our server arrived about 15 minutes after we were seated, he simply asked, "Do you know what you want?" While he wasn't rude, and was attentive and friendly for the rest of the meal, it's not the norm at a "white table cloth" restaurant. Our food arrived in an appropriate time after we ordered. I had to add salt to my food. I do not like salty food, and I actually don't even own a salt shaker in my house, but the spaghetti carbonara lacked any flavor, what so ever. The most flavorful part of the dish were the english peas. My partner also  begrudgingly added salt to his meal, because the tomato sauce was flat and tasteless. We didn't have any cocktails, and after the dinner skipped dessert.< /Review>

<userid>115081486968594133629</userid>< Review>
So I've lived here almost 14 months so far -

Pros: Location, Amenities (Gym, Pools, etc), Friendly Staff (Leasing, Maintenance, Security and otherwise)

Cons: Fire Alarm, Door/FOB (maid access), Blinds (need to install white/blackout combo blinds vs transparent white only), Washer & Dryer (IrvineCo - time to get a deal with LG or Samsung, come on :)

I have not listed noise as an issue for me - as a person that is home 90% of the time, since I typically just work from home -- it has not been an issue for me during that day.  It really has not even been an issue for me during the night.

Every now and then I do hear a little boom shaking noise like my neighbor is lifting weights or something above me haha - but to be honest I've grown used to it and it is so infrequent it doesn't bother me.

I feel like people writing negative reviews based on noise have unrealistic expectations.  If you are not OK with a little noise then you probably shouldn't live in such close quarters.

To be honest I've had loud music playing and some people over a few times and security has been out a small % as well to politely ask us to lower it, but we are always respectful once someone has reached out either directly or indirectly.

Perhaps I'm lucky - as I feel the amount of noise complaints on me have actually been quite low... so I'm not sure if my direct neighbors are on the same wave length as me and are able to deal with each others minor noise generation levels.

Also I've no idea what people are complaining about with parking -- there is two garages with guest parking as well as the assigned parking spots all seem empty to me for the most part.

Anyways - I'm generally happy here - there were some frustrating moments in the beginning, but the staff has always been friendly and with the exception of the issue in regards to my maid not able to obtain her own FOB for her entry of which she is accustomed to from my prior location - forcing me to leave my door open most of the time, but hey - I haven't been robbed yet either.

So all in all I guess I've really just had an entirely different experience then some of these other reviewers.  I think you'll be happy as long as you appropriately manage your expectations.< /Review>

<text>Great place.  I've been a long time fan of Tokyo Garden and Miyoshi is the same owner and in a lot of ways like a second location.

The Sushi here and at Tokyo Garden is by far the best in Bakersfield.  I've tried almost every sushi place in town and even ventured outside of Bakersfield in a quest to find good sushi.  By far, you can't get much better than this.

One detail I love is that they don't put some mayonnaise / imitation crab meat slurry in their rolls.  Next time you go somewhere and order a roll that has crab meat in it, take a look and you'll notice that it's not sliced peaces inside but instead it's a bunch of mayo mixed together with finely minced crab meat and stuffed inside there.  Not here and not at Tokyo Garden.

For me it's the little details that matter and this place does it right down to the smallest fraction.< /text>< Pictures>

<text>I don't know about the people that have left bad reviews because I've had nothing but consistent excellent service for six years now. <text>1...2...3... Strikes and you're out.

My girlfriend and I are from Phoenix, AZ, and this was hands down the most disappointing sushi we have ever had. Despite all the great reviews, miyoshi failed to deliver on any front. From the interesting (to put it nicely) service experience to the food, we were disappointed. We only ordered basics, and they failed there, making us afraid to try one of the more expensive rolls.

First strike:
Miso soup 0 out of 5 : Tasted like brine water that was left to reduce all day... Missing ingredients and even spoons.

Second strike:
California roll 1 out of 5 : seriously, how do you mess up a cali roll? Its krab salad, cucumber and avocado... Rice was not cooked right and ingredients were bland and almost tasteless.

Third strike:
Spicy tuna roll 1 out of 5: again, rice fell apart and pretty tasteless.

Summary:
Every restaurant we have tried is AZ has been better. Would not recommend. Seriously, it was bad...< /text>< rate>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
Yeah, this place rocks. Obviously you aren't here for the atmosphere, you're here for the burger, and this one is superior. Excellent toasted bun, fresh toppings, good, flavorful beef. The fries were crispy and the portions substantial. Seems like the garlic on them was slightly sauteed, instead of the usual raw garlic bite.
Wish I could have tried the milkshakes, but I was stuffed with the burger and fries. Glad I didn't get an extra pattie, despite the quality.

The restaurant is kind of hard to spot in the dark, unless you know what you are looking for.</Text>

Good burgers as usual, but minus one star for service with an apparent two-faced, bi-polar attitude. We waited about 5 minutes before anybody noticed us. Cashier finally came out of the kitchen after chatting with the cook, and was  very pleasant when we first came in, but after we paid for our order, she went back into the kitchen and was talking and laughing with the cook again. Not a word about where to wait, just that she would let us know when it was ready. When she came back in a few minutes, and saw we were still standing there, and rather abrasively barked at us to "Hey! wait outside, we can't just have people waiting around in here. Covid, you know." After  stepping outside, we saw a customer who had  been sitting outside at a patio table come in to request a drink refill and the cashier not only served him immediately, but chatted with him for 2-3 minutes after. A warning to all: if you order takeout here, be prepared to step outside IMMEDIATELY after ordering or you will get chewed out. The cashier was  pleasant again when she brought our order, spouting compliments,  but that was little recompense for her attitude earlier. I agree with supporting local small business, but I do NOT agree with poor treatment of customers, and attempting to patronize  them afterward as if nothing happened.< /Review>

<Time>1554519159207</Time>< Review>
For about $8 you can get a single cheeseburger, fries, and a drink. A drive thru quarter pounder meal costs more than that. Despite constant mixups with orders delivered to the wrong table, the food arrived quickly. I would have to guess J's Burgers is trying to emulate the Double-Double folks with the style and ingredients on the burgers. Includes shredded lettuce, tomato, and onion. The difference is J's uses their own sauce, which is tasty, but a bit watery. (makes a mess by the time you get to the end of the burger). The fries are shoe string thin, way too greasy, and don't taste very good, just like the other guys. Limited soda fountain drinks.
They also offer kids meals, chicken sandwiches, onion rings, and milkshakes.
Convenient location on Spring Street with a tiny parking lot shared with the shoe store everyone loves to hate.
Open late-ish compared to other locally owned places.<//Review>

<Rate>5</Rate>< review>
Small hole-in-the-wall burger joint next to Takkens. Small menu, mostly burgers & fries. I've visited twice and ordered a double cheeseburger each time, and they were both absolutely delicious. The service was good and they cooked the food fast. As of April 2016, the double cheeseburgers are only $4.85, about the same price as fast food but infinitely tastier. If you're looking for a real, hand pressed burger but don't want to spend a lot, this is the place. Will keep coming, and would recommend to anyone.</review>
